In addition to the relatively far location, there is a Wanda Plaza that can solve the dining problem for more than ten minutes by car. The environment and facilities of the entire hotel are very good. I believe in the quality of Hyatt. I recommend this if you have a car in Badaling.

msg:I have always liked Hyatt, a tall hotel brand. This trip is no exception. The Hyatt Regency Shanghai Expo has a magnificent architecture and an excellent location. It is less than a 10-minute drive from Yanqing Railway Station and is only one road away from the entrance of Expo Park 2.
When I checked in, I was told that my room was upgraded to the fifth floor. From the balcony of the room, you can overlook the entire hotel garden and the Yongning Pavilion of the World Garden Park.
The hotel staff are warm and attentive. When I encountered a problem, from the lobby manager to the receptionist at the front desk, they were patient and meticulous to help me solve the problem.
The lights in the hotel rooms are all sound-controlled, which is convenient and energy-saving.
The toilet and shower in the room are separate. The toilet has a flushing function, which is convenient and hygienic.
In addition, the cleaning lady in the hotel room was also very polite and provided enough bottled water every time.
At noon on the day of arrival, I chose to dine in the hotel‚Äôs Chinese restaurant. The dining environment was very comfortable. I tasted the cold wild pine sprouts for the first time. The taste is very good. Wasabi shrimp balls, oil-pour noodles, etc. are also very delicious, a pleasant dining experience.
In contrast, the breakfast is indeed somewhat insufficient. There are not too many types to choose from, the wonton wrapper is too thick and hard. Even if there are few people in the off-season, there should be a basic level. Breakfast is not only a belly wrap, but also the beginning of a good mood for the day.
If the hotel has a swimming pool, it will always be a plus for me. The swimming pool water is very clear and the swimming is very enjoyable. The disadvantage is that the shower plumbing is somewhat clogged, causing the water to be unsmooth.
In general, staying at the Hyatt Regency World Garden is a great experience.
